+Super Item Modifier {<I>With This Code, Go Into Any Item Menu, And Position The Cursor Next To The Item You Wish To Change. Hold R3, And Press The Buttons Indicated Above, And The Item Will Be Replaced With The Next Or The Previous Item In The Hierarchy (E.G., The Next Best Sword, Or If You&#39;Re On The Best Sword, The Worst Spear, Etc.). You Have To Release And Depress The The Start Or Select Buttons In Order For The Cycle To Work, Holding Down Both Buttons Won&#39;T Work. Yes, That&#39;S Deliberate. Allowing That Would Cause The Items To Cycle Almost Faster Than You Can See, And Certainly Faster Than You Can React, And Any More Elaborate Handling Of The Button Presses Would Just Add Tons Of Lines To The Code. This Is Confirmed Working In The Shop Menus, The Item And Warehouse Menus, The Equipment Screen, And The Hospital. It Will Not Work In The Bonus Menu For Obvious Reasons (No Cursor). The Item Must Exist For It To Be Changed. That Is To Say, You Can&#39;T Change Slots Labeled With The (None), (Weapon), (Other), Etc. Placeholders. Just Buy A Cheap Item And Go To Work On It. Oh Yeah, And The Items Are Created Afresh Each Time You Come To Them. That Means Different Specialists And Rarity. So If You Come Across One You Like, You Probably Should Stop. On The Other Hand, If You Hit One That&#39;S Kind Of A Dud, You Can Just Advance One And Go Back. All The Variable Data Will Be Generated Again.</I>}

+All New Items Specialists Modifier Quantity Digits {<I>With This Code, Go Into Any Item Menu, And Position The Cursor Next To The Item You Wish To Change. Hold R3, And Press The Buttons Indicated Above, And The Item Will Be Replaced With The Next Or The Previous Item In The Hierarchy (E.G., The Next Best Sword, Or If You&#39;Re On The Best Sword, The Worst Spear, Etc.). You Have To Release And Depress The The Start Or Select Buttons In Order For The Cycle To Work, Holding Down Both Buttons Won&#39;T Work. Yes, That&#39;S Deliberate. Allowing That Would Cause The Items To Cycle Almost Faster Than You Can See, And Certainly Faster Than You Can React, And Any More Elaborate Handling Of The Button Presses Would Just Add Tons Of Lines To The Code. This Is Confirmed Working In The Shop Menus, The Item And Warehouse Menus, The Equipment Screen, And The Hospital. It Will Not Work In The Bonus Menu For Obvious Reasons (No Cursor). The Item Must Exist For It To Be Changed. That Is To Say, You Can&#39;T Change Slots Labeled With The (None), (Weapon), (Other), Etc. Placeholders. Just Buy A Cheap Item And Go To Work On It. Oh Yeah, And The Items Are Created Afresh Each Time You Come To Them. That Means Different Specialists And Rarity. So If You Come Across One You Like, You Probably Should Stop. On The Other Hand, If You Hit One That&#39;S Kind Of A Dud, You Can Just Advance One And Go Back. All The Variable Data Will Be Generated Again.</I>}
